style="background-color: #eee"><td colspan="2" class="infobox-full-data"><div style="text-align: left;">Sources: Polish <a href="/wiki/Aeronautical_Information_Publication" title="Aeronautical Navigation">EUROCONTROL</a><sup id="cite_ref-AIP_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AIP-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><br />Statistics from Office of Civil Aviation<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p><b>Katowice Airport</b> (<a href="/wiki/Polish_language" title="Polish language">Polish</a>: <i lang="pl">Mi\xc4\x99dzynarodowy Port Lotniczy Katowice</i>) (<a href="/wiki/IATA_airport_code" title="IATA airport code">IATA</a>: <b>KTW</b>, <a href="/wiki/ICAO_airport_code" title="ICAO airport code">ICAO</a>: <b>EPKT</b>) is an <a href="/wiki/International_airport" title="International airport">international airport</a>, located in <a href="/wiki/Pyrzowice" title="Pyrzowice">Pyrzowice</a>, 30&#160;km (19&#160;mi) north of <a href="/wiki/Katowice" title="Katowice">Katowice</a>, <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a>. The airport has <a href="/wiki/List_of_airports_in_Poland" title="List of airports in Poland">the 4th-biggest annualy passenger flow in Poland</a>. Katowice Airport is the biggest <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Polish</a> airport in terms of <a href="/wiki/Air_charter" title="Air charter">leisure</a> traffic.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> It is also the second biggest airport in the country in terms of <a href="/wiki/Cargo" title="Cargo">cargo</a> traffic. It operates a variety of charter, regular and cargo flights. <a href="/wiki/Long-haul_flights" class="mw-redirect" title="Long-haul flights">Long-haul flights</a> are operated from Katowice to <a href="/wiki/Canc%C3%BAn" title="Canc\xc3\xban">Canc\xc3\xban</a> in <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mal%C3%A9" title="Mal\xc3\xa9">Mal\xc3\xa9</a> in <a href="/wiki/Maldives" title="Maldives">Maldives</a> and to <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Plata,_Dominican_Republic" title="Puerto Plata, Dominican Republic">Puerto Plata</a> as well as <a href="/wiki/Punta_Cana" title="Punta Cana">Punta Cana</a> in <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">Dominican Republic</a> by <a href="/wiki/LOT_Polish_Airlines" title="LOT Polish Airlines">LOT\'s</a> <a href="/wiki/Boeing_787_Dreamliner" title="Boeing 787 Dreamliner">Boeing 787s Dreamliner</a>. The airport has the tallest <a href="/wiki/Air_Traffic_Control" class="mw-redirect" title="Air Traffic Control">Air Traffic Control Tower</a><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> and the second longest <a href="/wiki/Runway" title="Runway">runway</a><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> in <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a>. Katowice Airport is the <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland\'s</a> only airport with more than one passenger terminal and the airport with the biggest number of based <a href="/wiki/Airlines" class="mw-redirect" title="Airlines">airlines</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> The Katowice Airport serves the most industrialised region in Poland, one of the most urbanised areas of Europe. 13 million inhabitants are estimated to live within 100 km of Katowice Airport. This is a larger catchment area than many airports in Europe.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2 tocsection-22"><a href="#Accidents_and_incidents"><span class="tocnumber">6</span> <span class="toctext">Accidents and incidents</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-23"><a links</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_years">Early years</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early years">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The current location of Katowice Airport was initially used by <a href="/wiki/Germans" title="Germans">German</a> <a href="/wiki/Soldier" title="Soldier">soldiers</a>. In 1940, the <a href="/wiki/Luftwaffe" title="Luftwaffe">Luftwaffe</a> began construction of an airbase in the meadows around Pyrzowice. The Germans built three stone and concrete airstrips, with runway lengths varying from 1,000 to 1,500 meters, all of which around 50 meters wide. The airbase was used for handling of military aircraft flying from the inner part of the <a href="/wiki/German_Reich_(1933%E2%80%931945)" class="mw-redirect" title="German Reich (1933\xe2\x80\x931945)">German Reich</a>, carrying supplies to <a href="/wiki/Troops" class="mw-redirect" title="Troops">troops</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Front_(World_War_II)" title="Eastern Front (World War II)">Eastern Front</a>.\n</p><p>In the final phase of <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Messerschmitt_Me_163_Komet" title="Messerschmitt Me 163 Komet">Messerschmitt Me 163 Komet</a> rocket-powered aircraft were tested here. Following General <a href="/wiki/Ernst_Udet" title="Ernst Udet">Ernst Udet</a>\'s (a Luftwaffe <a href="/wiki/Flying_ace" title="Flying ace">flying ace</a>) death in 1941, the airfield was named <i>Udetfeld</i>.\n</p><p>From 1945 to 1951, <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Air_Forces" title="Soviet Air Forces">Soviet soldiers</a> were stationed at the airbase. In the early 1950s, the Soviets handed the airbase over to the <a href="/wiki/Polish_Air_Force" title="Polish Air Force">Polish Air Force</a>. It was then used by the 39th Fighter Regiment, created on 17 April 1951.\n</p><p>A new runway was built in 1964. Soon after, the airbase Pyrzowice became host to its first-ever regular passenger traffic, when on 6 October 1966, the first plane of LOT Polish Airlines took off for Warsaw. By the end of 1969, a small passenger terminal was built (550 m<sup>2</sup>), together with a taxiway and an apron.\n</p><p>This runway has since been replaced by a new adjacent one (3,200m), completed in May 2015.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Development_since_the_1990s">Development since the 1990s</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Development since the 1990s">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>In 1991, G\xc3\xb3rno\xc5\x9bl\xc4\x85skie Towarzystwo Lotnicze (GTL) (English: Upper Silesian Aviation Group) was created. On 27 March 1993, the German carrier Lufthansa flew to <a href="/wiki/Frankfurt_Airport" title="Frankfurt Airport">Frankfurt Airport</a>, thus inaugurating the first international service.\n</p><p>Passenger Terminal B officially opened in 2007, followed by (arrivals only) Terminal C, in 2015.\n</p><p>Future plans include the construction of a completely new passenger terminal, a further expansion of the recently built cargo terminal, and a new railway connection.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>On 3 October 2018, the airport celebrated 4 million passengers travelling through Katowice in a single year.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Facilities">Facilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Facilities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Pyrzowice_Katowice_Airport_noc.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Pyrzowice_Katowice_Airport_noc.JPG/240px-Pyrzowice_Katowice_Airport_noc.JPG" decoding="async" width="240" height="160" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Pyrzowice_Katowice_Airport_noc.JPG/360px-Pyrzowice_Katowice_Airport_noc.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2f/Pyrzowice_Katowice_Airport_noc.JPG/480px-Pyrzowice_Katowice_Airport_noc.JPG 2x" data-file-width="6016" data-file-height="4000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Pyrzowice_Katowice_Airport_noc.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Terminals A &amp; B at night</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Katowice-Pyrzowice_Airport_2016_10.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Katowice-Pyrzowice_Airport_2016_10.JPG/240px-Katowice-Pyrzowice_Airport_2016_10.JPG" decoding="async" width="240" height="180" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Katowice-Pyrzowice_Airport_2016_10.JPG/360px-Katowice-Pyrzowice_Airport_2016_10.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Katowice-Pyrzowice_Airport_2016_10.JPG/480px-Katowice-Pyrzowice_Airport_2016_10.JPG 2x" data-file-width="3264" data-file-height="2448" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Katowice-Pyrzowice_Airport_2016_10.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The longest viewing terrace in Europe in Terminal B (now under renovation)</div></div></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Terminals">Terminals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Terminals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/Airport" title="Airport">airport</a> features three passenger <a href="/wiki/Airport_terminal" title="Airport terminal">terminals</a> A, B (departures) and C (arrivals) as well as a cargo terminal. Operations at terminal B, much bigger than A, started on 30 July 2007. Terminals are capable of handling about 8.0 million passengers annually.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Terminal A handles all non-<a href="/wiki/Schengen_Area" title="Schengen Area">Schengen</a> departure flights, while Terminal B handles all <a href="/wiki/Schengen_Area" title="Schengen Area">Schengen</a> departure flights. The operation of the newest Terminal C building (arrivals) started on 27 June 2015. This terminal handles all arrival flights from non-<a href="/wiki/Schengen_Area" title="Schengen Area">Schengen</a> and <a href="/wiki/Schengen_Area" title="Schengen Area">Schengen</a> zones. Terminal B (departures to Schengen area) is under renovation (2019-2021) and is going to become on of the most modern terminals in Europe.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> The longest airport observation deck in Europe was able to be found inside the previous version of Terminal B. Terminal <a href="/wiki/Cargo" title="Cargo">Cargo</a> is located at the east of the airport and is one of the newest cargo terminals in the World.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> New passenger Terminal D is under planning such as new Cargo Terminal and Cargo City. New Terminal D will be equipped with jetways etc. There is a chance for Kiss&amp;fly zone and VIP Terminal in the future.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Runway_and_apron">Runway and apron</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Runway and apron">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The airport\'s concrete <a href="/wiki/Runway" title="Runway">runway</a> is 3200m by 45m, oriented 9 and 27, and can accommodate aircraft as large as <a href="/wiki/Boeing_747" title="Boeing 747">Boeing 747</a> or <a href="/wiki/Boeing_777" title="Boeing 777">Boeing 777</a>, albeit not at <a href="/wiki/Maximum_Takeoff_Weight" class="mw-redirect" title="Maximum Takeoff Weight">MTOW</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> Heavy transports such as <a href="/wiki/Antonov_An-124" class="mw-redirect" title="Antonov An-124">Antonov An-124</a><sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> or <a href="/wiki/Antonov_An-225" class="mw-redirect" title="Antonov An-225">An-225</a><sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> have been noted to land there on occasions. The airport uses new generation <a href="/wiki/Instrument_Landing_System" class="mw-redirect" title="Instrument Landing System">Instrument Landing System</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Thales_Group" title="Thales Group">Thales</a> 420 system.<sup id="cite_ref-ils_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ils-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> The runway at Katowice Airport is the second longest runway in Poland, behind <a href="/wiki/Warsaw_Chopin_Airport" title="Warsaw Chopin Airport">Warsaw Chopin</a>\'s runway 15/33. 33 new aircraft stands are under construction as of now. They will be located between taxiways E (Echo) and H (Hotel), to the west from main apron, between main and cargo apron and to the east from cargo apron.\n</p><p>The airport has two plane spotter stands, one at the western end of the airport\'s runway. The platforms are free to access.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Air_traffic_control_tower">Air traffic control tower</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Air traffic control tower">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The new <a href="/wiki/Air_traffic_control" title="Air traffic control">ATC tower</a> has been already built. It is the tallest ATC in Poland and in Eastern Europe, at 46 meters height.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Hotel">Hotel</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Hotel">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>A <a href="/wiki/Marriott_International" title="Marriott International">"Moxy by Marriott"</a> hotel has been built recently, and is now ready to accept guests. It is located right next to the main parking entrance (P1), very close to the terminals. A direct bridge connection to the terminals is also planned.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Car_parks">Car parks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Car parks">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>There are three main car parks at Katowice International Airport. P1, P2 and P3. P1 is the nearest parking connected direct with terminals. P2 is located to the east to P1. P3 is next to P2 and it is a guarded car park. There is a lot of private car parks next to the airport.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> The airport offers 3922 own parking spaces.<sup id="cite_ref-auto10_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto10-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> There is also Premium Parking at Katowice International Airport. P1 will be expanded to 1842 parking spaces by January 2019. It will be expanded to the west.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Maintenance">Maintenance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Maintenance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>At the airport are two main active <a href="/wiki/Aircraft_maintenance" title="Aircraft maintenance">maintenance buildings</a>. The first serves mainly <a href="/wiki/Wizz_Air" title="Wizz Air">Wizz Air</a>\'s aircraft, and the modern one belongs to Linetech and serving all other airlines. The second building is serving mainly <a href="/wiki/Embraer" title="Embraer">Embraer</a>\'s aircraft from all over the World.\n<br />Wizz Air\xe2\x80\x99s new maintenance hangar is under construction and is going to be ready in the end of 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> The building will be operated only by <a href="/wiki/Wizz_Air" title="Wizz Air">Wizz Air</a> and will be serving <a href="/wiki/Airbus_A321neo" class="mw-redirect" title="Airbus A321neo">Airbus A321neo</a> aircraft.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>\n<br />Due to the great conditions of the airport (long <a href="/wiki/Runway" title="Runway">runway</a>, huge three <a href="/wiki/Airport_apron" title="Airport apron">airport aprons</a>, many stands), Katowice Airport is home to 9 based <a href="/wiki/Airlines" class="mw-redirect" title="Airlines">airlines</a>. This is the biggest number of based airlines in <a href="/wiki/East-Central_Europe" title="East-Central Europe">East-Central Europe</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Airlines_and_destinations">Airlines and destinations</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Airlines and destinations">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Passenger">Passenger</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Passenger">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The following airlines Poland</a>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n</center>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ground_transportation">Ground transportation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Ground transportation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="By_car">By car</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: By car">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>The airport is accessible to/from <a href="/wiki/Katowice" title="Katowice">Katowice</a> and other cities of the region like <a href="/wiki/Cz%C4%99stochowa" title="Cz\xc4\x99stochowa">Cz\xc4\x99stochowa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Krak%C3%B3w" title="Krak\xc3\xb3w">Krak\xc3\xb3w</a>, <a href="/wiki/Opole" title="Opole">Opole</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gliwice" title="Gliwice">Gliwice</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kielce" title="Kielce">Kielce</a>, <a href="/wiki/O%C5%9Bwi%C4%99cim" title="O\xc5\x9bwi\xc4\x99cim">O\xc5\x9bwi\xc4\x99cim</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tychy" title="Tychy">Tychy</a> via <a href="/wiki/Expressway_S1_(Poland)" title="Expressway S1 (Poland)">Expressway S1</a>, <a href="/wiki/National_roads_in_Poland#List_of_national_roads" title="National roads in Poland">national road 86</a>, <a href="/wiki/A4_autostrada_(Poland)" title="A4 autostrada (Poland)">A4 motorway</a>, <a href="/wiki/National_roads_in_Poland#List_of_national_roads" title="National roads in Poland">national road 94</a>, <a href="/wiki/National_roads_in_Poland#List_of_national_roads" title="National roads in Poland">national road 78</a> and <a href="/wiki/A1_autostrada_(Poland)" title="A1 autostrada (Poland)">A1 motorway</a>. The airport is also served by <a href="/wiki/Taxi" class="mw-redirect" title="Taxi">taxis</a>, <a href="/wiki/Uber" title="Uber">Uber</a> and iTaxi. The airport offers 3,922 parking spaces.<sup id="cite_ref-auto10_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto10-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> There is also premium parking at Katowice International Airport. Car rentals are available.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="By_bus">By bus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: By bus">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>There are three bus lines (AP1, AP2, AP3) to Katowice Airport direct from Katowice, Tychy, Gliwice, Zabrze, Chorz\xc3\xb3w, Sosnowiec, B\xc4\x99dzin, Piekary \xc5\x9al\xc4\x85skie, Siemianowice \xc5\x9al\xc4\x85skie or Miko\xc5\x82\xc3\xb3w.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> Ride from airport to Katowice City Centre with this bus takes about 1H.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Flixbus" title="Flixbus">Flixbus</a> connects Katowice International Airport with <a href="/wiki/Katowice" title="Katowice">Katowice</a>, <a href="/wiki/Krak%C3%B3w" title="Krak\xc3\xb3w">Krak\xc3\xb3w</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cz%C4%99stochowa" title="Cz\xc4\x99stochowa">Cz\xc4\x99stochowa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chorz%C3%B3w" title="Chorz\xc3\xb3w">Chorz\xc3\xb3w</a> or <a href="/wiki/Bytom" title="Bytom">Bytom</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>Matuszek bus corporation connects Katowice Airport with <a href="/wiki/Katowice" title="Katowice">Katowice</a> city centre and <a href="/wiki/Krak%C3%B3w" title="Krak\xc3\xb3w">Krak\xc3\xb3w</a> city centre.<sup id="cite_ref-auto6_107-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto6-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>P-Air PyrzowiceEkspres.pl (official <a href="/wiki/WizzAir" class="mw-redirect" title="WizzAir">WizzAir</a>\'s carrier) connects the airport with <a href="/wiki/Krak%C3%B3w" title="Krak\xc3\xb3w">Krak\xc3\xb3w</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cz%C4%99stochowa" title="Cz\xc4\x99stochowa">Cz\xc4\x99stochowa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-auto6_107-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto6-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Leo_Express" title="Leo Express">Leo Express</a> connects the airport with <a href="/wiki/Ostrava" title="Ostrava">Ostrava</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rybnik" title="Rybnik">Rybnik</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gliwice" title="Gliwice">Gliwice</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bohum%C3%ADn" title="Bohum\xc3\xadn">Bohum\xc3\xadn</a> direct from the airport.<sup id="cite_ref-auto6_107-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto6-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>Bus connections from other largest cities of the region, such as <a href="/wiki/Krak%C3%B3w" title="Krak\xc3\xb3w">Krak\xc3\xb3w</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Cz%C4%99stochowa" title="Cz\xc4\x99stochowa">Cz\xc4\x99stochowa</a><sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> and minibus - inter alia from/to <a href="/wiki/Opole" title="Opole">Opole</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-www.airport-lotnisko.katowice.pl_110-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-www.airport-lotnisko.katowice.pl-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-www.elotnicze.pl_111-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-www.elotnicze.pl-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Wroc%C5%82aw" title="Wroc\xc5\x82aw">Wroc\xc5\x82aw</a><sup id="cite_ref-www.airport-lotnisko.katowice.pl_110-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-www.airport-lotnisko.katowice.pl-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-www.elotnicze.pl_111-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-www.elotnicze.pl-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> are also available. Local buses connect to the city of <a href="/wiki/Bytom" title="Bytom">Bytom</a> where one can change for bus to Katowice.</li></ul>\n<p>Bus stops are next to Terminal C and Terminal B. They are about 10 metres from the terminal entrance.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="By_rail">By rail</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: By rail">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p>There is currently no passenger rail link to the airport but the building of a railway between Katowice and the airport is being planned. There will be new railways from <a href="/wiki/Siewierz" title="Siewierz">Siewierz</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tarnowskie_G%C3%B3ry" title="Tarnowskie G\xc3\xb3ry">Tarnowskie G\xc3\xb3ry</a> to Katowice International Airport.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Accidents_and_incidents">Accidents and incidents</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Katowice_Airport&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Accidents and incidents">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<ul><li>On 27 October 2007, a <a href="/wiki/Boeing_737" title="Boeing 737">Boeing 737-800</a> chartered by the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">UN</a> destroyed dozens of approach and landing lights whilst making a low approach.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> No passengers were injured, but the approach lights were out of service for three weeks.</li>\n<li>On 12 March 2013, <a href="/wiki/Travel_Service_Airlines" class="mw-redirect" title="Travel Service Airlines">Travel Service</a> Flight 7137, a <a href="/wiki/Boeing_737" title="Boeing 737">Boeing 737</a>, overran the runway while landing in snowy weather just before 19:00, its nosewheel getting stuck approximately 3 feet deep into the soft ground 20 metres beyond the runway. None of the 176 passengers and 6 crew suffered any injuries, but the airport was closed until 17:00 the next day until the aircraft was recovered and taxied away.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>On 5 July 2014 <a href="/wiki/Lufthansa" title="Lufthansa">Lufthansa</a> Flight 1360, operated by <a href="/wiki/Lufthansa_Cityline" class="mw-redirect" title="Lufthansa Cityline">Lufthansa Cityline</a> landed on the new runway, under construction then. No passengers ended up injured, and the aircraft later made a technical flight to land on the original runway, as the new runway still had not been joined by taxiways to the taxiway system.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span href="/wiki/Katowice" title="Katowice">Katowice</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Silesian_Voivodeship" title="Silesian Voivodeship">Silesian Voivodeship</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Katowice_urban_area" title="Katowice urban area">Katowice urban area</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_airports_in_Poland" title="List of airports in Poland">List of airports in Poland</a></li></ul>\n<h2><span
